**HTTP Headers phÃ¢n loáº¡i:**

| Loáº¡i Header      | Headers                                                              |
| ---------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| General Headers  | `Cache-Control`, `Connection`, `Date`, `Pragma`, `Transfer-Encoding` |
| Entity Headers   | `Content-Type`, `Content-Length`, `ETag`, `Expires`, `Last-Modified` |
| Request Headers  | `Host`, `User-Agent`, `Accept`, `If-None-Match`, `If-Modified-Since` |
| Response Headers | `Server`, `Set-Cookie`, `Location`, `Access-Control-Allow-Origin`    |

#### Cache Rules: Expires vs Cache-Control

**Expires (HTTP/1.0):**

```
Expires: Thu, 01 Dec 2025 16:00:00 GMT
```

- LÃ  **thá»i gian háº¿t háº¡n tuyá»‡t Ä‘á»‘i**
- Server tráº£ vá» thá»i Ä‘iá»ƒm cá»¥ thá»ƒ cache sáº½ háº¿t háº¡n
- âš ï¸ **Váº¥n Ä‘á»**: Phá»¥ thuá»™c vÃ o Ä‘á»“ng há»“ client
  - Náº¿u client/server lá»‡ch mÃºi giá» â†’ cache sai!
  - Náº¿u user Ä‘á»•i system time â†’ cache invalid!

**Cache-Control (HTTP/1.1) - Æ¯u tiÃªn cao hÆ¡n:**

```
Cache-Control: max-age=600   // Cache trong 600 giÃ¢y
```

| Value         | Meaning                                             |
| ------------- | --------------------------------------------------- |
| `public`      | Táº¥t cáº£ Ä‘á»u cache Ä‘Æ°á»£c (browser + CDN/proxy)         |
| `private`     | Chá»‰ browser cache (default)                         |
| `no-cache`    | Cache nhÆ°ng pháº£i validate vá»›i server trÆ°á»›c khi dÃ¹ng |
| `no-store`    | KHÃ”NG cache gÃ¬ cáº£ (sensitive data)                  |
| `max-age=xxx` | Cache trong xxx giÃ¢y (relative time)                |

**VÃ­ dá»¥ Response Headers:**

```http
HTTP/1.1 200 OK
Expires: Thu, 01 Dec 2025 16:00:00 GMT    â† Absolute time
Cache-Control: max-age=600                 â† Relative time (10 mins)
```

ğŸ“Œ **Cache-Control > Expires** (náº¿u cáº£ 2 cÃ³ máº·t, chá»‰ Cache-Control cÃ³ hiá»‡u lá»±c)

### JavaScript Coroutines

#### Sá»± PhÃ¡t Triá»ƒn cá»§a JS Async

#### Generator - CÆ¡ Cháº¿ Coroutine trong JS

```javascript
// Generator = Coroutine implementation trong JavaScript
function* foo() {
  console.log("foo start");
  a = yield 1; // â† Suspension point 1
  console.log("foo a", a);
  yield 2; // â† Suspension point 2
  yield 3; // â† Suspension point 3
  console.log("foo end");
}

const gen = foo();
console.log(gen.next().value); // foo start â†’ 1
console.log(gen.next().value); // foo a undefined â†’ 2
console.log(gen.next().value); // 3
```

#### Async/Await - Syntactic Sugar

```javascript
// async/await = Wrapper cá»§a Generator + Promise
async function getData() {
  try {
    const response = await fetch("/api/data"); // Pause
    const data = await response.json(); // Pause
    return data;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(error);
  }
}
```

### Comparison Table

| Feature          | Process                | Thread                 | Coroutine             |
| ---------------- | ---------------------- | ---------------------- | --------------------- |
| **ÄÆ¡n vá»‹**       | Resource allocation    | Task execution         | User-level function   |
| **Memory**       | Isolated (riÃªng)       | Shared (chung)         | Shared                |
| **Overhead**     | High                   | Medium                 | Very Low              |
| **Creation**     | Slow                   | Fast                   | Very Fast             |
| **Scheduling**   | OS Kernel (Preemptive) | OS Kernel (Preemptive) | User (Cooperative)    |
| **Switching**    | Costly (system call)   | Less costly            | Almost free           |
| **Crash**        | Isolated               | Affects process        | Affects thread        |
| **Memory usage** | ~MB                    | ~8MB (Java)            | ~2KB (Goroutine)      |
| **Multi-core**   | âœ… Yes                 | âœ… Yes                 | âŒ No (single-thread) |
| **Best for**     | CPU-intensive          | General                | I/O-intensive         |

## 11. CÃ¢u Há»i Phá»ng Váº¥n

### Quick Reference

```
URL TO PAGE:
1. URL â†’ 2. DNS Cache â†’ 3. DNS Resolve (UDP) â†’ 4. TCP Connect
â†’ 5. HTTP Request â†’ 6. Response â†’ 7. TCP Close â†’ 8. Render

RENDERING:
HTML â†’ DOM Tree â†’ Render Tree â†’ Layout â†’ Paint â†’ Composite
CSS â†’ CSSOM Tree â†—

REFLOW vs REPAINT:
â€¢ Reflow: Geometry change â†’ expensive, triggers repaint
â€¢ Repaint: Appearance change â†’ less expensive
â€¢ transform/opacity: Composite only â†’ cheapest!

CACHING:
â€¢ Strong: Cache-Control > Expires â†’ 200 from cache
â€¢ Conditional: ETag > Last-Modified â†’ 304 Not Modified

PROCESS/THREAD:
â€¢ Process: Resource unit, isolated memory
â€¢ Thread: Execution unit, shared memory
â€¢ Coroutine: User-space thread, lightweight
```

### CÃ¢u Há»i ThÆ°á»ng Gáº·p

**1. MÃ´ táº£ quÃ¡ trÃ¬nh tá»« nháº­p URL Ä‘áº¿n hiá»ƒn thá»‹ trang?**

> 8 bÆ°á»›c: Nháº­p URL â†’ Check DNS cache (browser/OS/router/ISP) â†’ DNS resolve (UDP) â†’ TCP 3-way handshake â†’ HTTP request â†’ Server response â†’ TCP 4-way close â†’ Browser render (DOM â†’ CSSOM â†’ Render Tree â†’ Layout â†’ Paint â†’ Composite)

**2. Reflow vÃ  Repaint khÃ¡c nhau tháº¿ nÃ o?**

> - **Reflow**: Thay Ä‘á»•i geometry (size, position) â†’ tÃ­nh láº¡i layout â†’ expensive
> - **Repaint**: Thay Ä‘á»•i appearance (color) â†’ váº½ láº¡i â†’ less expensive
> - Reflow luÃ´n trigger Repaint, nhÆ°ng Repaint khÃ´ng trigger Reflow

**3. LÃ m sao tá»‘i Æ°u Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh reflow/repaint?**

> - Batch DOM changes (cssText, className)
> - Avoid reading layout props in loops
> - Use transform thay vÃ¬ position
> - Use will-change Ä‘á»ƒ promote layer
> - Position: absolute/fixed cho animations

**4. Giáº£i thÃ­ch 304 Not Modified?**

> Khi strong cache háº¿t háº¡n, browser gá»­i If-None-Match (ETag) hoáº·c If-Modified-Since. Server so sÃ¡nh, náº¿u khÃ´ng thay Ä‘á»•i â†’ tráº£ 304 (khÃ´ng body), browser dÃ¹ng cache cÅ©.

**5. Cache-Control vs Expires?**

> - **Cache-Control**: Relative time (max-age=3600), Æ°u tiÃªn cao hÆ¡n
> - **Expires**: Absolute time, phá»¥ thuá»™c system clock, cÃ³ thá»ƒ sai

**6. Process vs Thread?**

> - **Process**: ÄÆ¡n vá»‹ cáº¥p phÃ¡t tÃ i nguyÃªn, memory riÃªng, crash isolated
> - **Thread**: ÄÆ¡n vá»‹ thá»±c thi, chia sáº» memory vá»›i threads cÃ¹ng process, crash áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng cáº£ process
